  W5  THE COST OF REBELLION IS PAID BY THE PEOPLE AROUND HER
      Blaidd's tragedy + Iji's death ARE the theme — defying the order kills the people who love you (cf. our faction-consequence, FFX Q68).
  W6  GATED BY WORLD-STATE, NOT MARKERS
      Radahn's gravity HOLDS THE STARS; kill him + a star literally falls and craters the map, opening the path — the gate is a cosmological FACT, reachable by several routes (cf. our world-state gating + multi-path design).
  W7  THE QUEST UNLOCKS A HIDDEN WORLD
      whole starlit civilizations beneath the map, unreachable any other way — the reward for the quest is WORLD (cf. our district's hidden depths).
  W8  THE ITEM-CHAIN AS RITUAL
      each object unlocks the next (a blade -> a statue that flips a dungeon upside-down -> a cursemark on her own discarded corpse -> a ring for her doll's finger) — the quest IS a spell being assembled (cf. our ritual/assembly quest design).
  W9  THE ENDING IS OFFERED, NEVER IMPOSED
      after the final boss, a summoning sign appears — take her ending or refuse it, having done everything (cf. our finale design; the ending you must choose).
  W10 "DISTANCE INSTEAD OF DOMINATION" — AN AMBIGUOUS LIBERATION
      the beloved "best" ending is deliberately unresolved — freedom, or abandonment to a cold dark? — "one of Elden Ring's most debated narrative paths" (cf. our Liberate's "terrible mercy," our no-clean-answer ethos). ===============================================================================

### #72  "LET GO, BEGIN AGAIN" / THE TRAP THAT TEACHES THE PLAYER (Fallout: New Vegas — Dead Money)
  W1  THE WHOLE THING IS FOUR WORDS ("Let go
      Begin again."): every character, mechanic, system + ending executes ONE idea — the tightest thematic unity in the canon (cf. Papers Please Q31, Citizen Sleeper Q65).
  W2  THE VAULT IS UN-LOOTABLE BY DESIGN — THE *PLAYER* LEARNS THE LESSON
      your own greed + frustration IS the teaching; the mechanic says what dialogue can't (cf. Spec Ops Q27, Inscryption Q53; the design that indicts you).
  W3  STRIP EVERYTHING AWAY (the reset AS the theme)
      all gear, companions + power gone — you must literally "begin again" from nothing (cf. our fold's generational reset, Hades/Rogue Legacy Q47/Q49).
  W4  THE HAZARD TRIAD (collar + cloud + resurrecting enemies)
      three systems, one feeling — a place you don't conquer, you SURVIVE + escape (cf. This War of Mine Q30, Sunless Sea Q66, our survival-dread).
  W5  EVERY COMPANION IS A DIFFERENT FACE OF THE THEME
      vanity-obsession, revenge-obsession, appetite-vs- control — "the story is better understood through them" (cf. Planescape/MotB Q12/Q64, our companions- as-argument).
  W6  THE VILLAIN IS BLIND TO HIMSELF
      Elijah is "as much a prisoner of the Sierra Madre as the people he's enslaved" + genuinely confused why the others succumb to greed — he thinks his obsession is NOBLE (cf. our Amalgamation/Network; the villain who can't see he's the theme).
  W7  TWO EXTREMES, BOTH WRONG (Dog/God)
      bottomless appetite vs fanatical control are the SAME failure; the answer is temperance — "everyone has a 'Dog' inside of him" (cf. our conscience system; the balance lesson).
  W8  THE BURIED FOUNDING MYTH (Sinclair/Vera)
      the one man who LET GO built the whole trap — the theme's origin story, hidden in logs you must dig for + reconstruct (cf. Obra Dinn/Golden Idol Q19/Q54, our [READ]).
  W9  THE BEST ENDING IS WALKING AWAY WITH NOTHING
      talk every companion into abandoning their obsession + leave the gold — "it was cathartic" (cf. Undertale Q28, our Pacifist Law; walking away as victory).
  W10 INVISIBLY SEEDED THROUGHOUT THE BASE GAME
      Elijah's fingerprints at HELIOS One, Dean Domino posters as "visual white noise," graffiti about a place "where people leave their hearts behind" — the DLC haunts the main game before you know it exists (cf. Ranni Q71, our fold-seeding). ===============================================================================

### #73  A FIXED DEATH, AN OPEN QUESTION / WHO DO YOU BECOME ON THE WAY OUT (Red Dead Redemption 2 — Art
  W1  THE ENDING IS FIXED — THE ONLY CHOICE IS WHO YOU ARE WHEN IT COMES
      no build or play saves him; the game asks the only question left — what do you do with the time? (cf. our fold; every dynast dies).
  W2  STRONG -> BROKEN, NOT WEAK -> STRONG
      a deliberate inversion — his body, faith, family + certainty are taken APART, and what's left underneath is the man (cf. our fold's stripping; the anti-power-fantasy).
  W3  THE DIAGNOSIS REFRAMES THE WHOLE GAME RETROACTIVELY
      one story beat re-colors 30 hours in BOTH directions — a wasted life behind, borrowed time ahead (cf. our long-arc revelations).
  W4  REPUTATION CASHES OUT AS YOUR DEATH SCENE
      honor doesn't change WHETHER he dies, it changes WHO dies — a peaceful sunrise vs a bullet in the head + spit on the corpse (cf. SH2 Q35, Cyberpunk Q63, our standing + finales).
  W5  THE HARM COMES BACK WEARING YOUR OWN FACE
      he catches TB from a dying man he BEAT for a debt — the disease IS the job; and the amends (pulling the widow's son from the mine) can't undo it (cf. our death-math/consequence).
  W6  THE TURN IS A QUIET CONVERSATION
      a nun telling him he was kind is the axis of a 60-hour game — not a set-piece (cf. our companions/writing; the small scene that turns everything).
  W7  HIS LAST GOAL IS SOMEONE ELSE'S FUTURE
      he spends his death buying the NEXT generation a chance + hands over his hat — the legacy move (STARTLINGLY our fold; cf. DQV Q69).
  W8  THE MIRROR
      TWO ANSWERS TO THE SAME COLLAPSE: Dutch CLINGS (one more score, forever, trapped by his own lies); Arthur, dying, OPENS UP — the doomed man grows, the "free" man calcifies (cf. Q01, our factions).
  W9  THE JOURNAL AS A READABLE INTERIOR
      hand-drawn sketches + private prose, always available — "designed to humanize the protagonist beyond gameplay" (cf. our [READ]/unrecorded-ledger).
  W10 HE SUBVERTS THE SERIES' OWN THEME
      the man who most embodies the cowboy myth doesn't die WITH the west — he dies as a man who CHOSE, the one thing the myth never allowed (cf. our theme/collapse). ===============================================================================

### #74  THE PROPHECY MIGHT BE A LIE / EARNING A DESTINY BY CONVINCING PEOPLE (Morrowind — the Main Ques
  W1  THE PROPHECY MIGHT BE FAKE — AND IT MIGHT NOT MATTER
      you may be "some schmuck who got really lucky"; the game refuses to resolve it (cf. our chosen-one skepticism, our self-made dynasty).
  W2  "WITHOUT THE HERO, THERE IS NO EVENT"
      prophecy doesn't make the hero — the hero makes the prophecy true by doing it; destiny is narration written after the fact (cf. our earned-standing).
  W3  THE FAILED PREDECESSORS
      a cavern of ghosts who were ALSO chosen, ALSO believed, and ALL died — the prophecy has a body count of believers (cf. our fold; the generations who tried before).
  W4  THE HISTORY IS CONTESTED + THE VICTORS WROTE IT
      two irreconcilable accounts of the founding crime; the state church is built on a lie it enforces + you dig the truth from suppressed texts (cf. our recorded- vs-unrecorded/[READ] + the Amalgamation's edited record).
  W5  YOU BECOME THE CHOSEN ONE BY CONVINCING PEOPLE
      seven factions must each personally NAME you — by quests, gifts, bribery, murder or diplomacy. Destiny is a political campaign (cf. our standing-as- progression-spine, Gothic/Mount&Blade Q51/Q61).
  W6  THE MENTOR IS GUESSING TOO (and then leaves)
      a skooma-addicted spy investigating whether you're real, who gets recalled and hands you the whole operation (cf. our faction handlers).
  W7  THE CURSE IS THE CURE (Corprus)
      you must deliberately catch the villain's divine plague — surviving it makes you immortal; you take the enemy's corruption INTO yourself to face him (cf. our Amalgamation- bargain/temptation).
  W8  THE VILLAIN ASKS IF YOU'RE REAL — AND YOU ANSWER
      yes / I'm the Empire's tool / I'm self-made / I don't know — the thesis resolved by a dialog tree, and the ending happens either way (cf. our finales + Megaton).
  W9  MANTLING ("walk like them until they must walk like you")
      acting the part hard enough MAKES it true — even the "fake" answer produces a real hero (cf. our BECOME finale + upbringing; identity as accumulated action).
  W10 THE REWARD IS RELEASE, NOT GLORY + YOU CAN BREAK THE WORLD AND STILL WIN
      Azura frees you FROM the prophecy; and if you murder a god, the game says "persist in the doomed world you have created" — and STILL gives you a hidden path to finish (cf. our finales + no-brick-wall). ===============================================================================

### #75  RECRUITED BY MURDER / THEY GIVE YOU A HOME, THEN BURN IT DOWN (Skyrim — The Dark Brotherhood)
  W1  THEY RECRUIT YOU BY NOTICING A MURDER YOU ALREADY DID
      no application — a letter that says "WE KNOW," then you wake up kidnapped. The faction found YOU (cf. our reputation-driven recruitment).
  W2  THE INDUCTION TEST *IS* THE JOB
      three hooded strangers, one contract, no evidence — and it doesn't matter who you pick, because the test is whether you'll kill ON COMMAND (cf. Sinnerman Q40, our conscience system).
  W3  YOU CAN DELETE THE ENTIRE FACTION IN THE FIRST FIVE MINUTES
      kill the recruiter, take the Empire's money, wipe out a 14-quest chain — with real rewards on both sides (cf. our Megaton law).
  W4  THE FAMILY IS THE POINT
      a hidden home with a riddle-door, a hearth, + a radiant-dialogue found family who talk to EACH OTHER — ten quests spent making you love a house (cf. Hades Q47, RDR2 Q10, our district-as-home).
  W5  THE SCHISM
      TRADITION VS PRAGMATISM: a dying institution's reformer vs its orthodoxy-made-flesh (a mad jester with a corpse in a box) — neither clean (cf. our faction web + Network).
  W6  THE DEAD GOD PROMOTES YOU OVER YOUR BOSS'S HEAD
      the newest recruit becomes, by sacred law, superior to the leader — and every crack in the family runs from that moment (cf. our standing/faction politics; the promotion as a wound).
  W7  THE BETRAYER'S MOTIVE IS LOVE OF THE FAMILY
      Astrid sells you out to SAVE the family from a path she couldn't control — a betrayal from fear, not malice (cf. our faction-leader design).
  W8  THE HOME BURNS + THE BETRAYER MAKES HERSELF YOUR CONTRACT
      she performs the Black Sacrament ON HERSELF ("I AM the Black Sacrament"), hands you the guild + the knife, and asks you to kill her (cf. our fold's loss + persistent-consequence; the best single scene in the questline).
  W9  THE ESCALATION IS ABSURD AND EARNED
      beggar -> bride -> a legendary chef's identity -> a poisoned state banquet -> a body-double -> the Emperor's warship. Each step is a set-piece with a different verb (cf. our quest factory + escalation design).
  W10 THE PAYOFF *BECOMES* THE NEW HOME
      20,000 gold for the Emperor; the rebuilt Sanctuary costs 19,000 — the reward for the arc is the home you rebuild with it (cf. our city-builder + reward economy). ===============================================================================

### #76  A PERSON MADE OF STOLEN MEMORY / WHO ARE YOU WHEN YOUR PAST WAS EDITED (Baldur's Gate 3 — Shado
  W1  HER PERSONALITY IS A THING THAT WAS DONE TO HER
      memories surgically removed by her own faith "so she would not betray" it; even her NAME is stolen — a constructed person built on an edited record of a real one (cf. our Amalgamation; the edited self).
  W2  THE REAL PERSON LEAKS THROUGH
      flowers, animals, mercy, a hatred of pointless cruelty — traits "at odds with her Sharran training" that the conditioning couldn't erase. You see her before she does (cf. our [READ]; the truth that survives the edit).
  W3  THE GOD KEEPS A WOUND IN HER
      an "old wound that never healed" is actually a LEASH that flares when she acts like her real self (cf. our Amalgamation's hold; control as pain).
  W4  THE ARC IS TRIGGERED BY THE *WORLD*, NOT A MENU
      a statue, a rescued child, an Insight check — her secrets surface from contact with things that hurt (cf. Cyberpunk Q63, our companions).
  W5  THE PLAYER'S ROLE IS PERMISSION, NOT PERSUASION
      the winning line is "Throw that spear away. MAKE YOUR OWN CHOICE" — you don't convert her, you give her the right to choose (cf. our companion-agency design).
  W6  PUSHING TOO HARD BACKFIRES
      arguing early makes it WORSE; patience is the mechanic (cf. our relationship design; restraint as skill).
  W7  BOTH PATHS FULLY BUILT, WITH REAL WORLD COST
      Dark Justiciar armour + a doomed refugee inn; or divine torture + silver hair + freedom — and you can lose her entirely (cf. our Megaton law).
  W8  THE FINAL CHOICE IS A TROLLEY WITH NO GOOD TRACK
      free her parents (they die) or she takes their curse (she suffers forever) — she finds her family and loses them either way (cf. our no-clean-answer ethos).
  W9  INTIMACY AS THE SYMBOL OF A RECLAIMED SELF
      she invites you to SWIM — the thing the church's stolen memory made her fear. Freedom expressed as a small, specific, human act (cf. Cyberpunk-Judy Q63, our writing).
  W10 THE DARK ENDING IS A REAL PERSON TOO
      she becomes Mother Superior, spreads Shar's word, ends the romance with a kiss "for old times' sake" — and pities the woman who broke her, "now able to understand what she went through." Damnation written with as much care as salvation (cf. our Megaton law). ===============================================================================

### #77  EVERYONE IS LYING, PICK ONE / THE CURE THAT COSTS YOU EVERYTHING YOU ARE (Cyberpunk 2077 — Phan
  W1  EVERY PARTY IS LYING, INCLUDING YOUR LIFELINE
      a president who wants a weapon, an honest man who's a government tool, a victim who's using you — no honest broker exists (cf. our faction web + Network).
  W2  YOU CANNOT NOT BETRAY SOMEONE
      no third option, no talk-out — and the cost lands within five minutes (a friend murdered, or your allies clocking your treachery) (cf. our Megaton law).
  W3  THE TWIST RE-READS YOUR BETRAYAL
      she was never going to cure you — the question flips from "who do I trust?" to "who am I, knowing nobody deserved it?" (cf. our Amalgamation's offer).
  W4  BOTH CASES ARE HONEST + IRRECONCILABLE
      a woman made into a weapon against her will vs a man who loves her and is right that she's dangerous — critics who played everything couldn't rank them (cf. our Megaton law).
  W5  THE OPPOSING BRANCH IS HOW YOU LEARN THE TRUTH
      side against someone and you get their backstory in flashback — then you're allowed to CHANGE YOUR MIND (cf. our faction web; the branch that teaches you).
  W6  A CHORUS WHO FRAMES THE THEME WITHOUT PREACHING
      Johnny names the system's logic ("once they've got their hooks in you, they'll never let you go") before the player can articulate it (cf. our companions + no-preaching rule).
  W7  THE CURE COSTS EVERYTHING YOU ARE
      you win — and wake from a two-year coma with your friend erased, your body unable to hold your trade, and a normal, boring life (cf. Hearts of Stone Q70; the wish granted exactly).
  W8  THE "TRUE" ENDING IS ALSO THE "WORST" ENDING
      both readings are defensible — it's the most connected + the most devastating (cf. our finales; ambiguity that survives the wiki).
  W9  THE CHOICE IS MADE WITHOUT KNOWING THE REPERCUSSIONS
      "every ending has you consider all the decisions you had the power to influence WITHOUT KNOWING what the repercussions would be" (cf. our fold's generational blindness — the deepest port).
  W10 MERCY AFTER BETRAYAL AS SELF-DEFINITION
      you can free the person who lied to you, gaining nothing — "the only right choice is the one that makes you feel the least regret" (cf. our Pacifist Law). ===============================================================================

### #78  A GOD IN A SUBURB / THE MERCY THAT IS A MASSACRE (Fallout 3 — Tranquility Lane)
  W1  A GOD MADE OF A LITTLE GIRL
      an omnipotent 200-year-old in a child's avatar, voice slipping between a girl's and an old man's, running a suburb as a torture-and-reset loop (cf. our Amalgamation; the god in the machine).
  W2  THE CHEERFULNESS IS THE WEAPON
      monochrome 1950s Americana + a chirpy loop under atrocity — "no less terrifying" than the wasteland; players end it just to stop the music (cf. DQV Q69, our Stardew-surface thesis).
  W3  THE CRUELTY LADDER WITH MULTIPLE SOLUTIONS
      make a child cry (punch him / convince him it's his fault / a brochure / kill his parents), break a marriage, murder a neighbor — an immersive-sim sandbox where every solution is monstrous (cf. our Megaton law).
  W4  YOUR FATHER IS THE DOG
      the man you've chased all game watches every atrocity, and you only learn it after (cf. our companions-as-witnesses).
  W5  YOU NEVER HAD TO DO ANY OF IT
      the failsafe is available from the start — every atrocity was optional; you obeyed because you were told to (cf. Dark Brotherhood Q75, Sinnerman Q40).
  W6  THE EXIT IS HIDDEN BEHIND THE VILLAIN'S OWN THEME SONG
      the failsafe code is the neighborhood's melody, which Betty herself whistles in the street — the way out is something you've been hearing all along (cf. our [READ]; the clue in plain hearing).
  W7  THE MERCY IS A MASSACRE
      the "good" option kills twelve people for real, because after 200 years of torture-and-reset, death is the only exit (cf. Dead Money Q72, our death-math).
  W8  A SELF-AWARE WITNESS
      one old woman knows it's fake, knows who Betty is, and begs you to end it — the only person in the world who can SEE it (cf. our [READ]/unrecorded truth; the one who remembers).
  W9  THE PUNISHMENT FITS PERFECTLY
      the unkillable god gets eternity alone in an empty suburb with nothing to torment — worse than death, by his own design (cf. our Amalgamation's fate options).
  W10 THE RECORD OUTLIVES THE PERSON
      the vault terminals still politely report "***RESIDENT REQUIRES IMMEDIATE MEDICAL ATTENTION***" over twelve corpses (cf. our [READ]/records). ===============================================================================

### #79  A ROCKET TO HEAVEN / COMEDY THAT EARNS SINCERITY (Fallout: New Vegas — Come Fly With Me)
  W1  AN ABSURD PREMISE PLAYED COMPLETELY STRAIGHT

  W2  THE CRUELTY IS INSIDE THE PUNCHLINE
      the funniest character is a delusional man whose labor was exploited by the kindest-seeming one, who knew he'd be left behind (cf. Hearts of Stone Q70).
  W3  EVERY OBSTACLE HAS A NON-VIOLENT SOLUTION (all missable)

  W4  BELIEF WRITTEN WITH RESPECT, NOT MOCKERY
      a prophet who genuinely believes, whose flock named him, and whose kindest line is "every feral ghoul you spare now is one that we can save later" — and it's MECHANICALLY TRUE (cf. our faction web; faith taken seriously).
  W5  THE TOWN LUNATIC IS THE RELIABLE WITNESS
      "commie zombies who want to hijack rockets and paint Lenin's face on the moon" is nonsense, and approximately correct (cf. our [READ]; the unreliable source who's right).
  W6  THE ERRANDS ARE A WORLD-TOUR WITH MULTIPLE SOLUTIONS
      buy/steal/lockpick the modules; loot the fuel or realize the CHILDREN'S TOY ROCKETS contain it (cf. our quest factory).
  W7  THE CHOICE IS BETWEEN TWO KINDNESSES
      take a man's delusion and give him a town, or let him keep it and die happy — "neither was a great choice" (cf. our Megaton law + Amalgamation's comfort-vs-truth).
  W8  THE INVISIBLE KINDNESS
      a hidden skill check lets you land the pilgrimage 12.5% CLOSER — nobody thanks you, and it changes the ending slides (cf. our Pacifist Law + optional-depth).
  W9  YOU CAN LOOT A RELIGION
      murder the whole cult, or farm their space suits — the game never stops you (cf. our Megaton law).
  W10 IT WAS THE FIRST QUEST DESIGNED FOR THE GAME
      the studio's opening statement of intent — every conflict talkable, every faction human, every joke load-bearing (cf. our design pillars). ===============================================================================

### #80  WHO HOLDS THE REINS OF HISTORY / A POLITICAL EPIC WHERE THE HEROES REFUSE THE WEAPON (Final Fan
  W1  THE GODS ARE HISTORIANS + THE PLOT IS A FIGHT OVER THE PEN
      immortals who pick kings + write history, called "the true weavers of history" — the whole war is about who holds the record (cf. our Amalgamation, Morrowind Q74).
  W2  THE VILLAIN'S PLOT IS EMANCIPATION
      a rogue god commits class treason + leaks god-power to humans so they can be free of gods; the mad scientist "seeks power not for its own sake, but to free mankind" (cf. FFX Q68, PSIII Q67, our faction web).
  W3  THE HEROES WIN BY REFUSING THE WEAPON

  W4  THEY WEAR HER DEAD HUSBAND TO STEER HER

  W5  THE WORLD IS THE PROTAGONIST
      "the party is simply a small cog"; an ecosystem, not a theme park; the villains are better-developed than the party, ON PURPOSE (cf. Gothic/Kenshi Q51/Q55, our district).
  W6  THE GAMBIT SYSTEM
      players PROGRAM their party's AI with prioritized If/Then macros — "automate the mundane and focus on macro-strategy"; the most robust party-AI system ever shipped (cf. our scheduler + entity AI).
  W7  EVERY FACTION IS A DIFFERENT ANSWER
      a queen and an emperor with the SAME goal; a Napoleon who takes the crown from the pope; a father who broke the world for his kids; a church that's a rubber stamp (cf. our 13 factions).
  W8  THE THESIS IS PROVED BY RESTRAINT, NOT A SPEECH
      six of seven have cause to nuke the empire, and the means, and they refuse — disproving the gods' claim that humans need a leash, silently (cf. our PACIFIST LAW + no-preaching rule).
  W9  THE PAYOFF LANDS 1,000 YEARS LATER
      the victory's meaning resolves in a different game, where a mortal changes history alone BECAUSE the leash was cut (cf. our ~100-year fold).
  W10 THE AUDIENCE-SURROGATE AS DELIBERATE ARCHITECTURE
      a POV character who doesn't understand the politics so the politics can be explained — a real technique, correctly identified, that half-worked (cf. our fold's new generations; and see the flaw). ===============================================================================

### #81  THE MAN THEY ERASED / HISTORY IS WRITTEN BY THE CHURCH THAT WON (Final Fantasy Tactics)
  W1  THE GAME IS A SUPPRESSED DOCUMENT
      a scholar centuries later finds papers hidden in the church's vault and asks you to help decide if the official hero is the real one — every battle is a reconstruction of a censored record (cf. our [READ] + recorded-vs-unrecorded).
  W2  THEY ERASED THE HERO AND EXECUTED THE ARCHIVIST
      five years of writing the truth, burned as heresy to protect the church's corruption — the record is the real battlefield (cf. our Amalgamation/Network).
  W3  IT WAS BORN FROM A REAL ECONOMIC COLLAPSE
      Matsuno built it from Japan's bubble bursting — "an era when many were robbed of hope, when dreams were measured by their price tag" (cf. our post-economic-collapse premise).
  W4  PRIVILEGE IS SHOWN IN A HOUSEHOLD
      the good father who still says, on his deathbed, that your brother is meant to be your SERVANT (cf. our faction/class politics).
  W5  THE ENEMY YOU'RE SENT TO CRUSH IS RIGHT
      the opening act is putting down a peasant rebellion whose goals your best friend "understands and shares" (cf. our factions).
  W6  MODERATION IS COMPLICITY
      "Ramza's determination to remain moderate in the face of social injustice cost at least one of his loved ones their lives" — and the class divide is exposed as ABSURD by a kidnapper who can't tell a noble from a commoner (cf. our conscience system).
  W7  TWO FRIENDS, TWO METHODS, BOTH SINCERE
      one fights beside the people and is erased; one manipulates everyone and is crowned — and they understand each other perfectly (cf. our faction web + finales).
  W8  EVERY POWER IS RUNNING A CON, AND THE CONS COLLIDE
      a "gambit pileup" where schemes wreck each other; a cardinal who doesn't believe in the god he sells (cf. our 13 factions).
  W9  THE FAITH STAT IS THE THEME
      belief is your magic power AND your vulnerability — "you can't not believe in attack magic without not believing in healing magic" (cf. our conscience system; theme as a number).
  W10 THE HERO NEVER RISES ABOVE SQUIRE
      saves the world, alters history, holds no rank, gets no statue (cf. our standing + fold). ===============================================================================

### #82  A MAN BUILT FROM A FALSE MEMORY / THE CITY THAT EATS BELIEF (Vagrant Story)
  W1  THE STATE BUILT A WEAPON OUT OF A FAKE MEMORY
      his defining grief is an edit — he killed the innocent family, and the guilt was installed to make him loyal (cf. our Amalgamation, Shadowheart Q76).
  W2  WHAT SURVIVES THE EDIT IS THE REAL MAN
      "the only thing that defines him is his REGRET of the killing of innocents, WHETHER THEY DIED BY HIS HAND OR NOT" — the conscience is true even when the memory isn't (cf. our [READ]; evidence over testimony).
  W3  THE CITY GIVES EVERYONE POWER AND WATCHES
      a ruin that hands magic to whoever enters — "none of the characters really take this well," some go drunk with power (cf. our Amalgamation + district).
  W4  "ON WHAT PRETEXT SHALL WE APPREHEND THEM?" / "WE NEED NO PRETEXT!"
      the state manufactures its justification on-screen in the first scene — and secretly FUNDS the cult it's raiding (cf. our Network + faction web).
  W5  THE HERESY IS THE OLDER FAITH
      the cult revives the religion the state church "once exterminated" — the heretics are the originals (cf. FFT Q81, our faction web + [READ]).
  W6  THE PIOUS MONSTER
      a paladin whose sincere faith is exactly what makes him capable of anything, fed by a power that won't let him stop (cf. FFT's Faith stat Q81).
  W7  THE VILLAIN'S TERRORISM IS A SUICIDE MISSION
      the whole crisis was staged to hand the world's most dangerous power to the one person who wouldn't use it — "he'd be a Well-Intentioned Extremist if he wasn't basically RIGHT ABOUT EVERYTHING" (cf. FFXII's Venat Q80, our faction web).
  W8  REMEMBERING IS THE LEVEL-UP
      Ashley starts as "a lifeless tool" and gains combat chains as his memories return — the progression system IS the theme (cf. our [READ] + fold + standing).
  W9  THE RUIN IS A REAL TOWN
      built from photographs of Saint-Émilion; the first dungeon is a wine cellar, and the wine's PRICE is still tracked (cf. our Vegas geography + economic premise).
  W10 HE WINS AND HISTORY CALLS HIM A MURDERER
      the prologue convicts him of the Duke's death before the story begins — the truth you played is the thing the record denies (cf. FFT Q81, our recorded-vs-unrecorded). ===============================================================================

### #83  EVERY PERSON HAS A BED / THE SELF-HELP CULT THAT ATE A KINGDOM (Ultima VII: The Black Gate)
  W1  EVERY NPC HAS A LIFE THAT ISN'T ABOUT YOU
      full daily schedules — wake, work, tavern, home, sleep — for EVERY character, not just plot ones; "they are there because they are" (cf. our district + entities + scheduler).

      no karma bar — just people who saw what you did, party members who QUIT, and companions who eventually ATTACK you (cf. our conscience system; the anti-karma answer).
  W7  THE COLLAPSE IS AMBIENT

  W8  THE VILLAIN BREAKS THE FOURTH WALL, WATCHES YOUR CRIMES, AND IS SECRETLY YOU

  W10 YOU GO UNDERCOVER, AND SO DOES THE PLAYER

### #84  THE SERVANT WHO BECOMES A PERSON / KILL GOD, THEN KILL YOURSELF SO NOBODY TAKES THE JOB (Dragon
  W1  THE PAWN SYSTEM — ASYNCHRONOUS COMPANIONS IN A SOLO GAME

      "not by defeating the bad guy pulling all the strings, BUT BY UNDERCUTTING THE SYSTEM ALTOGETHER... you're the FINAL savior, SO THAT NO OTHER SAVIORS CAN FOLLOW" (cf. our LIBERATE finale, Ranni Q71, FFXII Q80).

  W1  A-LIFE — THE WORLD RUNS WITHOUT YOU

  W1  THE THEME IS A MECHANIC THAT CANCELS ITSELF

      the game refuses a fail state — murder the plot and necromancy gives you a workaround, with companion barks written for it (cf. our no-brick-wall + [READ]).
  W7  PACIFIST TO GENOCIDE, BOTH FULLY BUILT
      talk through most of the main quest, or side with the villain and kill EVERY LIVING THING — then he betrays you anyway (cf. our PACIFIST LAW + Megaton law).
  W8  REPUTATION IS A MEMORY, NOT A BAR
      shopkeepers discount you, strangers cite YOUR SPECIFIC DEEDS by name, and companions join or refuse based on what you've actually done (cf. Ultima VII Q83, our standing).
  W9  THE FOUNDING MYTH IS A THEFT
      the father of the industrial age stole the steam engine from the dwarves, who are now the underclass it displaced (cf. our [READ] + faction web).
  W10 THE PUNISHMENTS DERIVE FROM THE PHYSICS
      resurrection is cheap and available to BOTH sides, so death is a slap and BANISHMENT is the real sentence (cf. our death-math + Amalgamation). ===============================================================================

### #87  YOU CANNOT DIE AND THAT IS THE PUNISHMENT / THE DEBT IS THE PLOT (Outward)
  W1  DEFEAT SCENARIOS INSTEAD OF DEATH
      losing triggers a STORY — captured and put to work in a mine, rescued by strangers, robbed, or occasionally HELPED with "a quest advancing unexpectedly" (cf. our death-math + fold).
  W2  IMMORTALITY IS SCARIER THAN DEATH
      "failure costs you something MORE PRECIOUS than a videogame life: IT COSTS YOU TIME" — heal, restock, repair, walk all the way back, and maybe fail again (cf. our 120-BPM tick + survival accounting).
  W3  THE AUTOSAVE IS THE ENFORCER
      constant saving removes the reload button, which is the ONLY reason defeat scenarios have teeth — "you never fail [in other RPGs]" (cf. our persistence-v1).
  W4  "WE WEAR OUR DEFEATS WITH PRIDE"
      the loss-log becomes the character — "this happened to me and this happened to me... BUT I AM STILL HERE" (cf. our fold + roguelite structure).
  W5  LOSING GENERATES YOUR NEMESIS FOR FREE
      the chief who mocked you, robbed you, and enslaved you becomes a kill-quest you accept with a grudge — with no Nemesis system (cf. Nemesis Q48, our persistent consequence).
  W6  THE OPENING QUEST IS A DEBT
      pay your BLOOD PRICE in five days or lose your house — an economic inciting incident in a fantasy RPG (cf. our post-economic-collapse premise + Vegas).
  W7  YOU DON'T GET STRONGER, YOU GET READIER
      no XP, no levels, no scaling — "the way a player must PREPARE for each [zone] is different" (cf. our standing + inventory).
  W8  THE BACKPACK IS A REAL DECISION
      drop it to fight well, and lose access to everything in it — including the spellbook you forgot you left inside (cf. our inventory macro/micro).
  W9  EVERY QUEST HAS A CLOCK, AND THE WORLD EXECUTES ON IT
      ignore the warning that your town will be attacked and "you'd come back to find it SACKED, ALL THE NPCs GONE, AND EVEN TRAINERS LOST" (cf. our 120-BPM tick + city-builder + scheduler).
  W10 THE FEATURE IS TEXT ON PURPOSE
      they need "A LOT" of defeat scenarios, one set per dungeon — "THAT'S WHY IT'S NOT A CUTSCENE OR SOMETHING. IT'S JUST A LITTLE BIT OF TEXT" (cf. our FACTORY LAW). ===============================================================================

### #88  THIS IS HOW YOU DIED / THE POWER GOES OUT ON A SCHEDULE (Project Zomboid)
  W1  THE GAME TELLS YOU THE ENDING BEFORE YOU START
      "These are the end times. There was no hope of survival. THIS IS HOW YOU DIED" — the only thing it says before loading you in (cf. our death-math + hardcore stance).
  W2  THERE IS NO "NEW GAME" BUTTON, BECAUSE "NEW INFERS HOPE"
      the menu itself refuses the word (cf. our ART PHILOSOPHY; theme in the UI).
  W3  GUARANTEED DEATH MAKES SURVIVAL MEAN SOMETHING
      "every extra day feels EARNED... even TINY victories become memorable because players understand HOW FRAGILE EVERYTHING TRULY IS" (cf. our fold + survival accounting).
  W4  THE APOCALYPSE IS A PROCESS WITH A CLOCK
      "ELECTRICITY EVENTUALLY FAILS. WATER SYSTEMS STOP FUNCTIONING. FOOD SPOILS. MEDICAL SUPPLIES DISAPPEAR" — the world gets quieter and more desperate on a schedule (cf. our THREE CURRENCIES + life-support buildings).
  W5  EMOTIONAL CONDITIONS ARE SURVIVAL STATS
      boredom, anxiety, and panic are tracked — panic cuts your melee damage, and unhappiness makes EVERY ACTION TAKE LONGER (cf. our medicine currency + survival accounting).
  W6  THE DEATHS ARE DOMESTIC AND SPECIFIC
      killed by a burglar alarm on your first window; killed by wet clothes → cough → noise → horde; eaten by a zombie hiding in a TOILET (cf. our death-math).
  W7  THE APOCALYPSE PROVIDES CONSTRAINT; THE PLAYER SUPPLIES NARRATIVE
      no plot, no NPCs, no cutscenes — "your story is written BY YOUR HABITS, YOUR PRIORITIES, YOUR MISTAKES" (cf. Dwarf Fortress Q45, our district).
  W8  THE WORLD EXPLAINS ITSELF THROUGH ITS OWN DYING MEDIA
      TV and radio broadcast the outbreak's timeline until the stations go dark and the power fails (cf. our [READ] + recorded-vs-unrecorded).
  W9  THE COMMUNITY INVENTED THE INHERITANCE
      the Skill Recovery Journal — transcribe your knowledge into a bound notebook before you die, and your next survivor finds it. "PASSING THE TORCH OF KNOWLEDGE" (cf. our FOLD).
  W10 THE MASCOT IS A CARTOON RACCOON
      the bleakest sim in the genre has Spiffo — "we do have a cute, furry orange raccoon TO COUNTERACT THE BLEAKNESS" (cf. our ART PHILOSOPHY + despair-with-hope). ===============================================================================

### #89  THE ROPE, NOT THE STICK / STRANGERS BUILT THE BRIDGE YOU'RE STANDING ON (Death Stranding)
  W1  THE ROPE, NOT THE STICK
      Kobo Abe's metaphor — early humans used STICKS to push threats away and ROPES to pull things close; "most games are about sticks... DEATH STRANDING IS A ROPE" (cf. our PACIFIST LAW).
  W2  OTHER PLAYERS BUILD YOUR WORLD, ASYNCHRONOUSLY, WITH NO SERVER SUBSCRIPTION
      ladders, bridges, roads, generators, and safehouses appear in your solo game (cf. Dragon's Dogma Q84, our fold + city-builder).
  W3  THE ONLY REWARD IS A LIKE, AND PEOPLE BUILD ANYWAY
      no material payoff — "the player is NOT REQUIRED to give their resources... YET THEY DO SO NEVERTHELESS" (cf. our city-builder + district).
  W4  THE HIGHWAY IS CROWDFUNDED BY STRANGERS
      no single player can afford the bridge, so waves of players each pay a piece and walk away, and later waves DRIVE ON IT (cf. our city-builder + fold + logistics).
  W5  THE TERRAIN IS THE BOSS
      you control BALANCE with the triggers; walking is the skill; "took something we never even think about in games and turned it into something that REQUIRES OUR ATTENTION" (cf. our 120-BPM movement law).
  W6  PATHS SMOOTH AS PEOPLE WALK THEM
      enough porters on one route and "A VISIBLE FOOTPATH WILL GRADUALLY FORM, SMOOTHING THE TERRAIN" for everyone after (cf. our district + street generation).
  W7  HELP ARRIVES AS OBJECTS, NOT MESSAGES
      Dark Souls says "try jumping"; Death Stranding leaves you AN ACTUAL LADDER (cf. our fold's inheritance + [READ]).
  W8  THE DEATH SCREEN IS A SOCIAL SPACE
      you drift in the Seam among the floating souls of other players and can TOUCH them to strengthen a connection before returning (cf. our death-math + AMALGAMATION).
  W9  STRANGERS' GHOSTS HELP YOU FIGHT
      "white, ghost-like figures... EMERGE FROM THE TAR" to throw you blood bags and grenades — they represent real players (cf. our combat dial + companions).
  W10 THE PREMISE AGED INTO PROPHECY
      a game where the hero is a delivery driver shipped four months before 2020 made delivery drivers "the most important people in the world" (cf. our logistics + premise). ===============================================================================

### #90  WE ACCIDENTALLY MADE A HORROR GAME / THE ENEMY IS A FEELING (Subnautica)
  W1  THEY REMOVED THE GUN AND ACCIDENTALLY BUILT HORROR
      "we wanted to make an open-world underwater game **WHERE YOU DIDN'T KILL CREATURES**"; fans told them they'd "accidentally made a horror game" — because what you can't kill is infinite (cf. our PACIFIST LAW).
  W2  THEY HELD THE LINE WHEN PLAYERS DEMANDED WEAPONS
      kept the "no killing the killer fish" rule and **tweaked fauna behaviour instead** — took the feedback, rejected the requested solution (cf. our verdict workflow + Paolo-decides law).
  W3  THEY NAMED THE FEELING, THEN ENGINEERED IT
      catalogued the six fears, found they'd triggered them by accident, and "**ONCE WE SAW THESE PSYCHOLOGICAL FACTORS AT WORK, WE FOCUSED ON THEM**" (cf. our ART PHILOSOPHY).
  W4  OXYGEN TAXES CURIOSITY, MATHEMATICALLY
      every meter down costs two — one to go, one to get back; the clock makes wanting to see more a calculation (cf. our survival accounting).
  W5  NO MAP, AND A BURNING SHIP FOR A COMPASS
      landmarks and positional audio only, with the wrecked Aurora on the horizon as both plot and navigation (cf. Morrowind Q37, our HD tile repo).
  W6  HAND-CRAFTED WORLD, PROCEDURAL CONTENTS
      "you can't teach an algorithm art direction" — the geometry is authored, the resource nodes aren't (cf. our tile repo + prefab factory).
  W7  THE STORY ARRIVES BY RADIO, JUST WHEN YOU'RE LOST
      distress calls drip-feed a plot into a storyless game — "just when you might be lost for things to do, it'll start pinging off" (cf. our quest factory + [READ]).
  W8  PROGRESSION IS DEPTH, NOT POWER
      every upgrade is ACCESS — "the game wants you to become sustainable, **so that you can better explore**" (cf. Outward Q87, our standing).
  W9  THE MUSIC EXISTS TO MAKE THE SILENCE WORSE
      "the endless silence of the depths hits harder than any soundtrack could... **the music serves nothing more than to make those silent moments more dread-inducing**" (cf. our music repo).
  W10 THE ARC IS TERROR → COMPETENCE → LOVE
      players cured their real phobias and got scuba certified; one finished the game and "**didn't want to leave... it was starting to feel like home**" (cf. our ART PHILOSOPHY + despair-with-hope). ===============================================================================

### #91  THE FIRE HAS TO BE FED WITH PEOPLE / GWYN WAS AFRAID OF US (Dark Souls)
  W1  THE WORLD RUNS ON A FIRE THAT EATS PEOPLE
      every age of light is bought by burning the strongest being alive, and the fuel is literally the souls you collected all game (cf. our AMALGAMATION + electricity).
  W2  THE PLAGUE IS THE SYMPTOM OF A WORLD HELD PAST ITS TIME
      the Undead Curse "REPRESENTS THE WORLD'S UNNATURAL STATE AS IT STRUGGLES TO MAINTAIN THE AGE OF FIRE — WITH THE NATURAL ORDER DISRUPTED, DEATH ITSELF BECOMES DISTORTED" (cf. our death-math + Amalgamation).
  W3  THE GOD'S NOBLE SACRIFICE WAS FEAR
      "**LORD GWYN TREMBLED AT THE DARK... IN DIRE FEAR OF HUMANS... LORD GWYN RESISTED THE COURSE OF NATURE**" — he burned himself to postpone HIS SUCCESSORS (cf. our AMALGAMATION + Network).
  W4  THE RELIGION IS A RECRUITMENT TOOL
      the Way of White "TEACHES US THE NOBILITY OF SACRIFICE," and Gwyn told his children to "shepherd the humans" — meaning "CONVINCE US THAT WE TOO NEED TO SACRIFICE OURSELVES" (cf. our CHURCH + faction web, Ultima VII Q83).
  W5  BOTH ADVISORS ARE KINGSEEKERS
      the rebel serpent isn't your friend — "BOTH OF THE PRIMORDIAL SERPENTS ARE KINGSEEKERS," one wants you in the fire, one wants you on a throne (cf. Phantom Liberty Q77, our faction web).
  W6  THE PROPHECY WAS WRITTEN BY THE BENEFICIARY
      a "vague prophecy" and a goddess who turns out to be an illusion, both keeping volunteers walking toward the furnace (cf. Dragon's Dogma Q84, our Amalgamation).
  W7  THE OPENING TELLS YOU EVERYTHING EXCEPT THE WHY
      the cutscene "SPELLS IT ALL OUT"; the only thing withheld is "WHY the Age of Fire is ending OR WHAT IS TO BE DONE ABOUT IT" (cf. our [READ]).
  W8  THE REFUSAL IS IMPLEMENTED AS WALKING OUT OF THE ROOM
      no cutscene, no dialogue — "leaving the boss arena without lighting the final bonfire" (cf. our LIBERATE finale, Dragon's Dogma Q84).
  W9  THE FINAL BOSS IS EVERYONE WHO SAID YES
      DS3's Soul of Cinder is "THE AMALGAMATION OF THE ESSENCE OF EVERY CHAMPION WHO HAS LINKED THE FIRE," fighting with every player's build (cf. our AMALGAMATION).
  W10 THE ONLY LORD STILL AT HIS POST HAS NO LEGS
      every other Lord of Cinder shirked the duty; the loyal one "either crawled here… OR HE SIMPLY NEVER LEFT" (cf. our fold + faction web). ===============================================================================

### #92  THE CURE IS THE DISEASE / EVERY FACTION IS A CHARACTER (Bloodborne)
  W1  THE CURE IS THE DISEASE
      a miracle blood that heals anything and turns you into a beast — and the institution kept selling it because "**THE COMMON PEOPLE WERE EXPENDABLE**" (cf. our MEDICINE currency).
  W2  THE INSTITUTION IS THE MONSTER
      "'health' for the Church is simply **PROLONGING THE DAMAGE TO KEEP THE DESPERATE DEPENDENT ON 'TREATMENT' ANOTHER DAY**"; the bureaucracy is "A SOULLESS IDEOLOGY MADE MANIFEST AND RUN AMOK" (cf. our CHURCH + NETWORK).
  W3  FACTIONS *ARE* THE CHARACTERS

  W4  THE APOCALYPSE IS A LAB-ETHICS DISPUTE WITH A CUSTOMER BASE
      the founder said be careful; the students heard "stop testing on OURSELVES" and **outsourced the guinea pigs to the public** (cf. our Network + Amalgamation origin).
  W5  THE DOCTRINE IS PRINTED ON THE UNIFORM
      "**MEDICINE IS NOT A MEANS OF TREATMENT BUT RATHER A METHOD FOR RESEARCH**" is a clothing item description (cf. our [READ] + inventory).
  W6  THEY SELL YOU THE PLAGUE *AND* THE CURE FOR THE PLAGUE
      the Church created the beasts, then established the HUNT and armed the hunters (cf. our faction web + medicine/resources currencies).
  W7  THE COSMIC HORROR IS ABOUT BABIES
      "**the theme of maternity in the world of Bloodborne is DARKER THAN IN ANY VIDEOGAME MEDIA BEFORE**" — every faction, every god, is trying to have a child (cf. our FOLD).
  W8  THE VICTIM IS PROUD
      the false doctor, forcibly impregnated by a god — "**IT FEELS AWFUL… BUT, IT PROVES THAT I'M CHOSEN. DON'T YOU SEE?**" (cf. our CHURCH + conscience system).
  W9  THE WHOLE GAME WAS AN INTERVIEW
      the Hunter's Dream exists "**TO SELECT AND NURTURE POTENTIAL CANDIDATES CAPABLE OF BECOMING ITS CHILD**" — you were auditioning (cf. Dragon's Dogma Q84, our fold).
  W10 EVERY FACTION THAT REACHED FOR THE GODS DIED OF IT
      worship, study, commune — "**EVERY FACTION HAS BEEN DESTROYED OR CORRUPTED BY THE ATTEMPT**," and the gods aren't even evil (cf. our AMALGAMATION). ===============================================================================

### #93  NO MORAL SYSTEM MEANS REAL MORAL DILEMMAS / TRUST IS THE RAREST RESOURCE (Rust)
  W1  NO MORAL SYSTEM MEANS REAL MORAL DILEMMAS
      "**there is NO MORAL SYSTEM IN THE GAME ASIDE FROM THE SYSTEM YOU TAKE INTO IT. SO YOU END UP WITH REAL ACTUAL MORAL DILEMMAS**" (cf. our conscience system, Ultima VII Q83).
  W2  TRUST IS THE ONLY RESOURCE WITH NO NODE
      wood is common, metal is findable, and "**TRUSTING THE WRONG PERSON CAN COST YOU EVERYTHING... BUT THAT'S WHAT MAKES THE RARE MOMENTS OF REAL TRUST SO REWARDING**" (cf. our faction web + standing).
  W3  EVERY STRANGER IS SCHRÖDINGER'S THREAT
      the naked with a bow "**might be trash… or the guy who one-taps you and steals your AK. NOBODY TAKES THE RISK**" (cf. our entities + district).
  W4  THE STARTING KIT IS THE THESIS
      a rock, a torch, and bandages that **only stop bleeding — they don't heal** (cf. our death-math + survival accounting).
  W5  THEY KILL YOU BECAUSE YOU HAVE NOTHING
      "**you had nothing. But in Rust, KILLING = VALIDATION... you're not a threat — YOU'RE A MOVING STRESS BALL**" (cf. our conscience system + faction web).
  W6  THE BASE IS A HOSTAGE, NOT A MECHANIC
      days of work, and "**your heart will pound as you return to your base... KNOWING THAT EVERYTHING COULD BE LOST IN AN INSTANT**" (cf. our city-builder + district).
  W7  A FIVE-MINUTE REVENGE STORY WITH A CATCHPHRASE, UNSCRIPTED
      "**'THIS IS A MESSAGE FROM MRZERO!' AND ONE-SHOTTED BIGMATT WITH A PICKAXE**"— one of the most memorable moments the writer had (cf. Nemesis Q48, our quest factory).
  W8  PLAYERS INVENT DIPLOMACY FROM NOTHING
      the sideways strafe and the shouted "**I'M FRIENDLY, I'M FRIENDLY**... **SOMETIMES THE LAST THING YOU'LL HEAR**" (cf. our district + faction web).
  W9  PLAYERS BUILD GOVERNMENTS NOBODY CODED
      "**PLAYERS ALSO ENGAGE IN DIPLOMACY, NEGOTIATE TRUCES, AND EVEN ESTABLISH MAKESHIFT GOVERNMENTS**"; identical code produces wildly different server cultures (cf. our 13 factions + city-builder).
  W10 THE GEAR CHANGES YOUR BEHAVIOR MORE THAN YOUR ODDS
      "**you DO FEEL more powerful, and dominating of others, once you possess more powerful weapons. BUT A ROCK WAS STILL PRETTY EFFECTIVE AGAINST ME WITH A BOW**" (cf. our combat dial). ===============================================================================

### #94  THE WAR STARTED WITH AN UNPAID BILL / TEN MONTHS TO EARN ONE BETRAYAL (EVE Online)
  W1  THE BIGGEST WAR IN GAMING HISTORY STARTED WITH AN UNPAID BILL

  W2  TEN MONTHS OF REAL FRIENDSHIP TO EARN ONE WORD
      agents infiltrated for ~10 months, one became the CEO's trusted second, and the go-word was "**NICOLE**" (cf. our faction web + companions).
  W3  THE CONTRACT WAS A CORPSE, NOT MONEY

  W4  ONE BETRAYAL RECALIBRATED AN ENTIRE SOCIETY
      "**EVERY CEO IN EVERY CORPORATION WOULD THINK TWICE ABOUT WHO THEY TRUSTED**" (cf. our conscience system + faction web, Rust Q93).
  W5  ESPIONAGE IS LEGITIMATE PLAY
      "**WHAT IN ANOTHER GAME WOULD BE CALLED CHEATING... IN EVE ONLINE IS SIMPLY PART OF THE METAGAME**"; the developers permit it "**ABSENT EXPLOITS**" (cf. our faction web + Network).
  W6  THE FACTIONS ARE LEGAL ENTITIES WITH BILLS
      corporations that are "**QUITE LITERALLY CORPORATIONS**," alliances with a 1-billion formation fee and a monthly maintenance bill (cf. our 13 factions + city-builder).
  W7  THE DEVELOPERS BUILT A PERMANENT MONUMENT FROM THE WRECKAGE
      "Titanomachy," a real site players can pilgrimage to, arranged "**IN A HAUNTINGLY BEAUTIFUL ARRANGEMENT**" (cf. our district + persistent consequence).
  W8  THE PLAYERS ELECTED A REAL GOVERNMENT
      single-transferable-vote elections, NDA access to internal materials, an annual summit in Iceland (cf. our faction web, Rust Q93).
  W9  FOUR CONDITIONS PRODUCE REAL STAKES
      the academic finding — "**ANARCHIC STRUCTURE, PLAYER COMMITMENT... MEASURABLE ECONOMIC VALUE, AND RISK ASSOCIATED WITH PERMANENT LOSS**" (cf. our death-math + Megaton law).
  W10 THE BANK WAS A CON, TWO YEARS BEFORE 2008
      Cally's EVE Intergalactic Bank took deposits, promised interest, and vanished with ~$170,000 (cf. our post-economic-collapse premise). ===============================================================================

### #95  THEY BROKE THE SPELL TO FIND OUT IF IT WAS REAL (The Last Wish, The Witcher 3)
  W1  THE QUEST IS A CONTROL EXPERIMENT ON A RELATIONSHIP
      they delete the magic that bound them "**TO SEE IF, ONCE THE SPELL WAS NO LONGER IN EFFECT, THE MAGIC BETWEEN THEM WOULD STILL PERSIST**" — she risks losing him to find out if she ever had him (cf. our AMALGAMATION + companions).

  W5  THE DEAD EXPERT IS THE WARNING, AND THEY IGNORE HIM

  W6  THE CLIMAX RE-STAGES THEIR FIRST MEETING

  W7  THE THIRD-PARTY NARRATOR TELLS THE TRUTH THE CHARACTERS WON'T

  W8  THE ANSWER IS "NOTHING HAS CHANGED," AND IT'S AMBIGUOUS ON PURPOSE
      "**SHE WAS EXPECTING TO FEEL DIFFERENT. BUT NOTHING HAS CHANGED**" — real love, residual magic, or habit? Unanswered (cf. our no-clean-answer + Megaton law).
  W9  THE REJECTION IS WRITTEN BETTER THAN THE ROMANCE
      "**THE TRUTH CAME AS A BRUTAL SHOCK TO YENNEFER, THOUGH SHE WAS NOT THE KIND TO LET THIS SHOW**" — and you still ride home together (cf. our companions).
  W10 LYING TO BOTH COSTS YOU BOTH
      profess love to Triss AND Yennefer and "**YOU'LL LOSE BOTH OF THEM**" — the game lets you do it and then charges you (cf. our conscience system + Megaton law). ===============================================================================

### #96  HAD TO BE ME / SOMEONE ELSE MIGHT HAVE GOTTEN IT WRONG (Priority: Tuchanka, Mass Effect 3)
  W1  THE PERPETRATOR IS THE ONE WHO FIXES IT

  W3  THE DEAL PAYS IN THE EXACT CURRENCY YOU NEED

  W10 YOU CAN SHOOT HIM IN THE BACK AND THE GAME MAKES YOU WATCH

### #98  THE EARTH WILL NOT ACCEPT HIM / YOUR FATHER LET THE PLAGUE IN ON PURPOSE (Isidor's Body, Pathol
  W1  YOU MISS THE INHERITANCE BY HOURS AND GET BLAMED FOR IT

      "**GO TO DEEP STORAGE TO FIND RECORDS ON THE VOLUNTEER ARCHIVE TERMINAL**" (cf. our AMALGAMATION + [READ] + recorded-vs-unrecorded).
  W10 THE TRUTH IS A TWO-BUTTON DECISION MADE ALONE
      "**THE RECORDING IS SOMEWHAT INCRIMINATING - DECIDE WHETHER YOU WANT TO DELETE IT NOW OR PLAY IT TO MIKHAILA**" (cf. our [READ] + conscience system + no-clean-answer). ===============================================================================

### #120  HE MADE HER LOVE HIM SO HER GHOST WOULD BE USEFUL (Deionarra, Planescape: Torment)
  W1  HE ENGINEERED HER LOVE AS A COMPONENT

### #123  TELL HIM HE'S NOT A MONSTER AND HE'LL BLOW UP THE ROCKET (Come Fly With Me, Fallout: New Vegas)
  W1  THE FAITH HAS A PARTS LIST

      escape from "**THE VIOLENCE AND BIGOTRY FROM HUMANS AGAINST GHOULS**" (cf. our faction web + standing).
  W3  THE ENGINEER IS A HUMAN WHO THINKS HE'S A CORPSE BECAUSE HE WENT BALD

  W4  THE PROPHET KNEW AND USED HIM

  W5  THE MERCY OPTION SHOWS UP IN THE PASSENGER MANIFEST
      "**EVERY FERAL GHOUL YOU SPARE NOW IS ONE THAT WE CAN SAVE LATER**" / "**ANY FERAL GHOULS THAT ARE NOT KILLED INSIDE REPCONN WILL JOIN THE 'GREAT JOURNEY'**" (cf. our PACIFIST LAW + persistent consequence).

  W8  THE TRUTH OPTION ONLY UNLOCKS ONCE YOU KNOW HE'S BEING USED
      "**MUST ASK JASON ABOUT CHRIS AND LEARN... THAT THEY PLAN TO LEAVE HIM BEHIND IN ORDER FOR THE SPEECH OPTION TO APPEAR**" (cf. our [READ] + conscience system).
  W9  THE KIND ANSWER CREATES THE BOMBER
      "**CHRIS WILL BE FURIOUS AND DETERMINED TO SABOTAGE THE LAUNCH**" (cf. our no-clean-answer + Megaton law).
  W10 THE BEST YOU CAN DO IS 12.5%
      "**EXAMINE THE DATA AND MODIFY IT SO THAT THEY LAND 12.5% CLOSER TO THEIR TARGET DESTINATION**" (cf. our despair-with-a-thread-of-hope + ART PHILOSOPHY). ===============================================================================

### #124  THE CURE IS UNDER HIS OWN HOUSE / HE WAS BUILT TO KILL HIS SISTER (The Underground Facility, Ni
  W1  THE MANSION IS A LID
      "**THE LAB WAS BUILT BY THE NATIONAL WEAPONS LABORATORY AS A WAY TO KEEP HALUA IN CHECK**" — the beautiful house exists to hold down the basement (cf. our district + AMALGAMATION).

      "**A LETTER FROM A WOMAN WHO USED TO WORK AT THE LAB, WHO TRIED HER BEST TO ACT AS A MOTHER TO THE SIBLINGS IN THE MIDST OF THEIR BEING EXPERIMENTED ON**" (cf. our [READ] + fold). ===============================================================================

### #125  "TALI: TREASON"
  W1  THE OBJECTIVE IS THE WEAPON
      The quest sends you to find evidence, and the evidence is not a key that opens a door — it is a loaded thing that has a target, and the target is the father of the woman standing next to you. The instant you learn what it says, the fetch quest becomes a moral object. No other quest in the trilogy turns an inventory item into a decision this cleanly. **The item does not unlock the ending. The item IS the ending, and you get to not use it.**
  W2  THE PUNISHMENT ARRIVES BEFORE THE VERDICT
      She is renamed *vas Normandy* in the first thirty seconds, in a friendly greeting, by her aunt. No combat, no roll, no fail state. A word changed and she lost her home. The board's decision is telegraphed by grammar. This is the single most economical piece of writing in the mission: **the trial's outcome is announced by how someone says hello.**
  W3  THE INSULT BECOMES THE IDENTITY
      She keeps *vas Normandy* forever. Through the entire third game, when every other quarian is *vas Rannoch*. The thing they did to shame her became the thing she is. **A punishment the character decides to keep is worth ten speeches about resilience.**
  W4  THE DUNGEON IS A CONFESSION, ORDERED
      The Alarei is not a level, it is an argument delivered in sequence: reckless orders, then the stated goal (retake the homeworld), then the personal logs (he did it for her), then the body, then his last message (a task assignment), then the full technical record. By the time the game asks you the question, it has already answered *why* — and the answer makes the truth harder to tell, not easier. **Structure the discovery so the motive lands BEFORE the crime does.**
  W5  HIS LAST WORDS TO HIS DAUGHTER ARE A WORK ORDER
      "Destroy the main hub, bring the data to Xen and Gerrel." No apology. No I love you that isn't wrapped in an instruction. The most devastating characterization of a father in the trilogy, delivered in one recorded log, and the game never comments on it. **Let the dead reveal themselves through what they thought was urgent.**
  W6  THE HEARING IS A FACADE AND YOU CAN LEARN THAT BY LISTENING
      Four admirals, four agendas, one of them presiding without recusing, none of them primarily interested in whether she did it. War party, slaver party, peace party, family friend. The verdict is a vote about the geth war. **The trial is a proxy fight, and Tali is the object being thrown.**
  W7  THE LEARNING REWRITES THE CLIMAX
      Do the optional walk and the Paragon speech becomes a different speech: not "she's a good person," but "you are abusing this hearing for political ammunition." Same button, same points, different scene. **Optional knowledge that changes the TEXT of the climax rather than unlocking a new one is the cheapest, highest-value reactivity in the genre.**
  W8  THE BEST OUTCOME IS PURCHASED WITH MERCY YOU DIDN'T KNOW YOU WERE BANKING
      Veetor spared from Cerberus in mission two. Reegar ordered to stand down instead of dying heroically. Neither flagged. Both show up in a courtroom hours later and testify — **and they beat the stat check.** You don't need Charm if you were decent to two people who couldn't help you at the time. **The best political capital in the game is people you were kind to when it wasn't useful.**
  W9  EVERY ENDING COSTS SOMETHING REAL AND THE COSTS ARE INCOMPARABLE
      Truth: she keeps her people, loses her father's name, loses you. Lie: she keeps her father's name, loses her people, and thanks you for it, and a species war stays on the rails. Speech: costs a stat, or costs nothing, and that's the flaw. **There is no currency that converts a name into a nation, and the game refuses to invent one.**
  W10 THE SECRET DOESN'T STAY SECRET AND THE GAME TELLS YOU IN AN EMAIL
      Daro'Xen digs through the Alarei herself, finds the research, and sends you a note saying you should have shared it and now you'll watch from a distance. **Your discretion protected a name, not a truth.** The most mature consequence in the mission is a piece of mail confirming that suppression is a delay, not a deletion — and it arrives after the reward screen, when you thought the quest was over. ---

### #126  "RAPHAEL'S DEAL / THE HOUSE OF HOPE"
  W1  THE DEVIL IS THE ONLY HONEST PARTY AND HE HONORS THE CONTRACT
      No trick, no subclause, no monkey's paw. He states the terms, states what he wants it FOR, delivers first, on trust, and at the end of the game **he does exactly what he said.** In an eighty-hour game full of liars, the devil is the one who keeps his word. **The horror is not being cheated. It's that you weren't.**
  W2  HE DELIVERS BEFORE YOU PAY
      The Hammer lands on signature. The Crown is owed on a thing that hasn't happened yet, to a person who doesn't have it, for a fight forty hours away. **A futures contract with a mortal, settled in advance, in good faith.** Nothing makes a devil more frightening than watching him take the counterparty risk.
  W3  REFUSAL COSTS NOTHING AND THAT IS WHY IT WORKS
      No ambush, no curse, no closed door. He waits in a brothel for the rest of the game. **The offer never expires.** Every hour you don't take it, you are choosing not to take it, again. A punished "no" is a trap you escaped. An unpunished "no" is a temptation that lives in the save file.
  W4  THE HOUSE IS PEACEFUL AND THE PEACE IS THE TENSION
      You can walk it, loot it, insult the staff, steal the gloves, read the archive. Nobody stops you. **It stays calm until you touch the one thing you came for, and then everything catches fire at once.** Tension built from permission, not threat. **The house isn't guarding the hammer. It's watching you decide.**
  W5  THE PRISONER IS NAMED HOPE AND THE HOUSE IS NAMED AFTER HER
      He tortured a woman for years and hung her name over the door. And she is still, sincerely, hopeful. That is not a pun. It is the thesis: **he keeps hope alive on the premises because a house with no hope in it cannot tempt anybody.**
  W6  YOU CAN USE HOPE AND LEAVE HOPE
      Ask where the Hammer is and she tells you, warmly, immediately, because you spoke to her. Then walk out. No stinger, no comment, no karma. **The cruelest available action is one unmarked dialogue option and a door.**
  W7  "I'LL COME BACK FOR YOU" IS NOT IN THE GAME
      The most human lie in the medium, and Larian did not write the button. There is freeing her, and not. **The verb that lets you feel decent while abandoning her does not exist.** Same family as Q118/Q122/Q123/Q125: the game removes the verb. **This is the sharpest instance in the entire questbook, because the removed verb is a COMFORT, not a cruelty.**
  W8  YOU PAY THE TOLL WITH THE PROCEEDS OF THE HEIST
      Helsik accepts Gauntlets of Hill Giant Strength, an artifact from the house you have not yet broken into. **You fund the burglary with the burglary.** Played completely straight, never winked at, and it means the door to Hell is openable by anyone who has already been through it.
  W9  THE MERCY SHOWS UP AND IT IS BAD AT ITS JOB
      Spare Yurgir in Act 2, in an unrelated building, for no reward. He shows up in Hell and fights the devil with you. **He misses a lot.** He is not good. He came anyway. **This is Q125 W8 and Q123's passenger manifest, third confirmation, and this version is better because the mercy is INCOMPETENT and still worth it.**
  W10 HE SINGS HIS OWN BOSS THEME AND YOU CAN SILENCE HIM
      A devil performs a musical number, with lyrics, at you, during his own murder, because he is a narcissist and this is his final act. Players got goosebumps or cringed hard; both reactions are correct and both are the point. **And Silence works on him.** Not a scripted option, just a spell doing what it says. **The counter to a narcissist's last performance is to take his voice, and it is in the spell list, and nobody labeled it.** ---

### #127  "HEARTS OF STONE / O'DIMM'S PACT"
  W1  THE DEVIL IS A LITERALIST, NOT A LIAR
      Every catastrophe in the expansion is a wish working exactly as worded. O'Dimm's terror is grammatical — he is what happens when the universe has a legal department. Paired with #126's honest buyer: the corpus now holds both honest devils, and neither ever needs to lie.
  W2  THE IMMORTALITY IS THE PUNISHMENT
      Olgierd got everything back and the caring removed — the contract's cost was delivered INSIDE its benefit. The monkey's paw with no visible twist: the wish was the curse, whole and entire.
  W3  THE THREE WISHES ARE THREE AUTOPSIES
      Fun (the brother), fortune (the feud), love (the wife): each task tours a thing Olgierd already destroyed by wishing. The fetch list is a guided walk through the debtor's wreckage.
  W4  THE GHOST WON'T LEAVE WHEN THE PARTY ENDS
      Vlodimir's one night curdles in real time — appetite outliving its allotment is the whole Everec family in one beat, and O'Dimm's one-word eviction shows the leash without raising the voice.
  W5  THE PAINTED WORLD IS A MARRIAGE'S FILE FORMAT
      Iris's memories as walkable dioramas: the quest stores a relationship as LEVELS. The corpus's best staging of [READ]-as-space since Q124's descent — and here the archive is a person who must consent to being closed.
  W6  THE RELEASE REQUIRES HER YES
      The rose can be taken, but the quest's true version asks Iris to let go — informed, awake, on her own terms. Pre-consented truth (Q119) inverted into pre-consented ENDING.
  W7  THE FINAL BOSS IS A READING TEST
      No sword touches O'Dimm. The challenge is riddle and recognition — the player wins by having paid attention to the world's whispers. Comprehension as combat, the questbook's thesis given a boss slot.
  W8  THE REWARD IS A WORDING PROBLEM
      Win the safe branch and O'Dimm grants YOUR wish — and the scene is a literacy exam where ambition is the trap. The quest ends by making the player draft a contract opposite a literalist. Nothing in the corpus prices language higher.
  W9  THE COLLECTOR ALWAYS WAITED
      O'Dimm never chases, never presses, never arrives early. Patience as omnipotence: the scariest thing a power can do is be comfortable with your schedule (cf. Q126 W3's unexpiring offer — the two patience designs bracket temptation and enforcement).
  W10 BOTH ENDINGS COST THE SAME MAN DIFFERENTLY
      Collected, Olgierd pays with his soul; saved, he pays by having to live as someone who did all of it and now feels again. The rescue is not a refund. The corpus's cleanest NO-CLEAN-SURFACE finale this side of Q124.

### #128  "ANJU & KAFEI"
  W1  THE CLOCK IS THE DUNGEON
      Keys are appointments; walls are other people's schedules; the map is a timetable. No quest in the corpus builds its entire challenge from WHEN.
  W2  EVERYONE KEEPS THEIR SCHEDULE INTO THE APOCALYPSE
      The postman delivers, the innkeeper checks in guests, the thief robs — the world ends in three days and everyone clocks in. Routine as courage, and as denial; the quest refuses to rule which.
  W3  THE MIDPOINT IS A WOMAN DECLINING RESCUE
      The pendant delivered, Anju chooses to stay in a doomed town for a maybe. The player enables the bravest decision in the game and is not consulted on it.
  W4  SHAME IS DEFEATED BY PUNCTUALITY
      Kafei's arc has no persuasion node — he is not talked out of hiding; he keeps an appointment as he is. Arrival is the apology.
  W5  THE WEDDING ASKS YOU TO LEAVE
      The quest's final beat excludes its player: the Couple's Mask is handed over and the door is closed. Witness, then absence — the reward includes being dismissed from it.
  W6  FAILURE IS AMBIENT
      Miss an hour and no screen tells you; the world just quietly holds its sadder configuration. The chain fails the way real plans fail: without ceremony.
  W7  THE PRIZE SURVIVES THE ERASURE AND THE MARRIAGE DOESN'T
      Rewind to save the world and only the mask and the player remember. The quest gives the player a memory with no witnesses — carrying it IS the reward's final form.
  W8  THE POSTMAN IS THE THESIS IN MINIATURE
      His final choice (flee vs finish the route) compresses the quest's whole argument about duty and terror into one uniformed man reading his own regulations for permission to be afraid.
  W9  HOPE TRAVELS BY MAIL
      The chain's crucial links are LETTERS with collection times — intimacy routed through infrastructure. The corpus's best marriage of logistics and longing (cf. Q101's supply-chain rescue: this is the supply chain OF a rescue of a marriage).
  W10 THE END OF THE WORLD ATTENDS A WEDDING
      The final hour's staging — vows under the falling moon — is the medium's cleanest statement that meaning is a thing people do at deadlines, not after them.

### #129  "TENPENNY TOWER"
  W1  THE EFFORTFUL DOOR IS THE TRAP
      The quest prices diplomacy highest — most nodes, most legwork, most patience — and detonates it. Effort is not virtue; the corpus's harshest single lesson about player self-congratulation.
  W2  THE MASSACRE IS PRE-ANNOUNCED AND UNHEARD
      Roy tells you, at the gate, on day one, in tone if not in terms. The foreshadowing is drowned out by a UI element (the karma stamp). A meter can make players deaf.
  W3  CONVERGENT BODY COUNTS, DIVERGENT SIGNATURES
      Doors two and three end in the same basement; the only variable is whose name is on the guest ledger and how long the lobby smelled like peace.
  W4  THE WRONGED PARTY DECLINES YOUR ARC
      Roy will not be the grateful beneficiary of your speech build. He had his own quest running the whole time, and yours was a component in it.
  W5  THE RETURN IS UNMARKED
      No objective sends you back; the truth is compensation-free archaeology (Q116's law, executed at settlement scale).
  W6  THE REGISTER OF THE AFTERMATH IS MILD
      Roy's breeziness outperforms any snarl; atrocity discussed in the tone of a satisfied tenant is the file's coldest instrument.
  W7  JUSTICE IS LEFT ENTIRELY PRIVATE
      Kill Roy after and no system blesses or bills it — the one moment the karma engine's silence works FOR the scene: the player's response has no exchange rate.
  W8  BIGOTRY IS ITEMIZED
      The gauntlet decomposes "the tower won't allow it" into fourteen individually arguable humans — prejudice rendered as a canvassing problem, door by door.
  W9  POWER IS INDIFFERENT, NOT HATEFUL
      Tenpenny's shrug — sure, let them in, whatever — is the quest's sharpest political note: the owner never needed the bigotry; he just never needed to oppose it either.
  W10 THE QUEST COMPLETES BEFORE IT ENDS
      "Quest Complete" fires at the handshake; the actual ending arrives weeks later, uncredited. The gap between the game's bookkeeping and the story's truth IS the design (and F1's razor: one fingerprint would have made it undeniable).

### #130  "PARANOIA / GLARTHIR"
  W1  THE CLIENT'S REALITY IS PLAYER-WRITABLE
      Reports are writes to a man's world-model, and the model has a body count. No quest in the corpus makes the pen this literal.
  W2  THE GAMEPLAY TEACHES THE TRUTH BEFORE THE FORK ASKS
      You WATCH the innocence for three days before any node lets you deny it — the tails are the evidence; the reports are the confession.
  W3  TRUTH COSTS THE TRUTH-TELLER
      Honest reports spend your standing in his ledger, not his theory's. The corpus's cleanest model of why people stop correcting the paranoid: correction is expensive and billed to the corrector.
  W4  THE LIE IS FRICTIONLESS AT POINT OF SALE
      Confirmation costs one dialogue click and pays gold; the invoice arrives days later with names on it. Fear-feeding priced exactly like real life: cheap now, catastrophic on delivery.
  W5  MAINTENANCE IS A BRANCH
      The stall — managing a sick man forever for coin, curing nothing, killing no one — is the quest's darkest mirror and it's just... available, unmarked, indefinitely.
  W6  THE HYPOTHESIS HAS NO NODE
      "What if you're wrong" is absent because HE has no slot for it; the option list is a psychograph. Interface as the client's mind.
  W7  THE HELP-VERB FIRES BLANKS
      "You need a healer" is true, kind, and useless — the quest lets decency be correct and ineffective at once, which almost nothing in the medium permits.
  W8  THE INSTITUTION'S MERCY HAS INSTITUTIONAL GRANULARITY
      The guard exit works and is exactly as gentle as a city watch gets: the honest price of outsourcing a sick man to public order.
  W9  THE MIDNIGHT STAGING IS THE DIAGNOSIS
      Chapel shadows, passed notes, dawn drops — the quest wraps you in the paranoid's dramaturgy until following his stagecraft feels like procedure. Form as contagion.
  W10 NOBODY HAS TO DIE AND SOMEONE USUALLY DOES
      Every corpse in every branch is optional and authored; the quest's violence is 100% player-written through an intermediary who believes you. Responsibility with one layer of laundering — and the laundering is the lesson.

### #131  "BOETHIAH'S CALLING"
  W1  THE MURDER WEAPON IS THE TRUST INTERFACE
      The command wheel — the game's grammar of loyalty — issues the summons to the pillar. Betrayal executed entirely in loyalty's UI: no quest in the corpus fuses mechanics and meaning tighter.
  W2  THE VICTIM IS CAST AT RUNTIME FROM WHOEVER LOVES YOU
      The sacrifice is a ROLE filled from the player's actual social graph — the .bq alias system's darkest proof-of-concept, shipped five years before our format adopted the idea.
  W3  THE HONEST DEVIL DEALS ONLY IN TRUST
      Strangers free, followers priced: Boethiah's economics state the theme with total clarity — the third honest devil in the corpus (Raphael buys, O'Dimm collects, Boethiah EXCHANGES), and this one's currency is the purest.
  W4  REFUSAL IS FREE AND THE ENTRY IS IMMORTAL
      The journal holds the offer forever: a to-do item made of a person, glancing up at you from the quest log for two hundred hours. Temptation as UI persistence.
  W5  THE LAST EXIT IS AT THE ALTAR
      The walk-back stays available past every point of decency — through the selection, the journey, the binding. Completion is chosen continuously, never slid into; the design maximizes ownership.
  W6  CONFESSION IS DENIED
      No node exists to explain, warn, or apologize — before, during, or via corpse. The betrayer carries it silent by interface law.
  W7  APPROVAL ARRIVES IN THE BORROWED VOICE
      Boethiah's congratulations through the dead follower's mouth: reward staging as final twist of the instrument. The cruelest single line-delivery mechanism in the corpus.
  W8  THE RAGE-VERB LANDS ON THE WRONG BODY
      You can attack the corpse-puppet and only desecrate your own price. The game leaves anger available and makes it grotesque — emotion honored and made useless at once (cf. Q130 W7's blank-firing help-verb: the pair covers kindness and fury, both true, both useless).
  W9  SELF-SACRIFICE IS NOT PURCHASABLE
      "Take me instead" has no node because the commodity is definitionally someone ELSE's gift to you. The removed verb IS the economic theory of the quest.
  W10 THE ARMOR IS WORN OVER IT FOREVER
      The Mail — hissing, black, excellent — is the quest's afterlife: every subsequent hour in it is spent inside the decision. Reward as permanent residence in your own worst act.

### #132  "THE ARL OF REDCLIFFE / CONNOR"
  W1  FOUR DOORS, FOUR CURRENCIES, NO EXCHANGE RATE
      A child, a volunteer, a supply run, an integrity: the menu prices in incomparables and refuses conversion. The corpus's cleanest architecture of Q125-W9's law.
  W2  THE MONSTER MADE A GOOD-FAITH DEAL
      Connor's bargain was LOVE plus power minus training — the quest's horror has no malice anywhere in its causal chain, only concealment and emergency.
  W3  THE MOTHER SETS THE PRICE AND IS THE CAUSE
      Isolde's hiding built the bomb; Isolde's life is offered as payment — cause and currency in one person, and the quest lets her insist.
  W4  THE GOOD ENDING IS HOMEWORK
      Door three is gated on knowing the world and spending the travel: mercy as logistics, competence as compassion's admission fee. No stat, no alignment — just whether you learned the setting.
  W5  EVERY OPTION HAS A LIVING ADVOCATE IN THE ROOM
      The parlor stages the deliberation with all voices present and arguing — the corpus's best-BLOCKED decision scene; the player chooses inside a functioning argument, not a menu vacuum.
  W6  THE VILLAIN QUOTES PRICES MID-EVICTION
      The desire demon negotiates while being removed — the counterparty that never stops trading converts even the rescue's final room into a market.
  W7  CONSENT DOESN'T CLEAN IT
      Isolde's yes is explicit, repeated, formal — and the ritual is still monstrous, and the scene plays it as both. Pre-consented death, priced honestly.
  W8  THE PERFECT CRIME IS AVAILABLE
      Deal with the demon, walk out a hero, and no system ever checks: the quest trusts the player with an unaudited secret (and the trust is the test).
  W9  THE EMERGENCY'S MENU LIES BY OMISSION
      The fork presents as binary-plus-horror; the clean door exists OFF-MENU for those who know to ask. The quest models how real crises hide their best options behind composure and information.
  W10 THE NIGHT EARNS THE QUESTION
      The militia battle — fishermen, oil, barricades — spends the quest's first act making the player DEFEND the community whose ruling family's secret caused everything. You bleed for the village before learning the castle owed it the apology.

### #133  "THE TASTE OF DEATH / NAMIRA"
  W1  RECRUITMENT BY OBSERVED TEMPERAMENT
      Eola pitches you because you walked into a corpse hall steady — the cult reads the PLAYER'S ACCUMULATED COMFORT with the game's own violence and names it kinship. The fourth wall doesn't break; it gets complimented.
  W2  THE ESCALATION IS UPHOLSTERED IN ROUTINE
      Investigate, chat, clear a dungeon, RSVP, escort, carve — every increment is a taught verb. The unthinkable arrives via the quest loop's own grammar.
  W3  THE EXIT IS FIRST
      Kill her at hello and it's over, free. Every subsequent step is priced in the distance from that door — momentum as the mechanism of complicity (the inverted Boethiah; the pair is a complete theory of exits).
  W4  THE CLIENT BECOMES THE CARGO
      The man who hired the investigation is the feast it ends in — the corpus's only quest-giver eaten by his own quest. Contract structure as dramatic irony.
  W5  THE LIE COSTS ONE SENTENCE
      The entire deception is a line about a blessing. The cheapness is the statement: trust's exchange rate against a stranger's word, measured exactly.
  W6  THE VICTIM MAKES SMALL TALK ON THE WALK
      Verulus chats amiably to his carver across half a map — the trust-walk with the trust on-screen the whole way (Q131's march, with a voice).
  W7  THE WARNING VERB EVAPORATES UNLOCATABLY
      There is no single step where "tell him" becomes impossible; the option thins by increments until it isn't there. Conscience's closing window rendered as interface drift.
  W8  THE RESCUE ARRIVES AT MAXIMUM AWKWARDNESS
      Flip the altar and you save a man you personally delivered — heroism with your own fingerprints on the table settings. The game permits it and prices it at the whole reward.
  W9  NO BACKSTORY IS OFFERED OR OBTAINABLE
      Eola's hunger has no origin node; the design refuses the etiology that would let the player file and dismiss her. Unexplained appetite is the scarier species.
  W10 THE REWARD KEEPS ASKING
      The Ring of Namira only does anything when fed — the quest's residue is a standing invitation in the inventory, renewable nightly, forever. The afterlife of the act is a mechanic with your hand in it.

### #134  "THE HOUSE OF HORRORS / MOLAG BAL"
  W1  THE TRAP RUNS ON GENRE TRAINING
      You entered because abandoned houses are content. The god's lure is the player's own loop — no bait needed beyond a door being slightly open (cf. Q133 W1: the Daedric pair reads the PLAYER; Namira reads your calm, Bal reads your habits).
  W2  THE FIRST PAYMENT PRECEDES THE TERMS
      Tyranus dies before Bal introduces himself — you're in debt before the negotiation opens, and the debt is a body. Contract law as ambush.
  W3  THE GOD IS PATIENT FROM INSIDE THE ROOM
      No timer, no escalation, no punishment for refusal — just a door that stays a wall. Pressure as pure subtraction: everything removed except compliance.
  W4  MARTYRDOM ISN'T STOCKED
      The noble exit has no node; the god of domination doesn't sell that item. The removed verb IS the theology.
  W5  THE RESCUE FRAME DELIVERS THE VICTIM
      Standard rescue verbs — find, free, escort — retrieve a prisoner for his torturer, playing completely straight. The corpus's darkest reuse of a benign quest grammar (Q131's UI-betrayal law, quest-loop edition, second confirmation with Q133).
  W6  PRIDE COMPLETES THE LURE
      Tell Logrolf the truth and he comes anyway, to defy. The quest lets honesty and outcome fully decouple — clean mouth, identical hands.
  W7  THE REPETITION IS THE POINT
      He submits; Bal demands it AGAIN. Domination defined mechanically: not the yielding but the re-yielding — the quest teaches the concept through a second button-press that feels entirely different from the first.
  W8  THE REWARD ARRIVES MID-SWING
      The mace restores in your grip during the beating — payment materializing while the arm still moves. Complicity's receipt printed in real time.
  W9  THE HOUSE FORGETS YOU INSTANTLY
      Door opens, Markarth resumes, no one asks. The seamless re-entry into the ordinary is the quest's last cruelty: the world's indifference co-signs the act.
  W10 THE ONLY REFUSAL IS REAL
      The single genuine no — abandoning the quest forever — costs the player something actual (the open journal entry, the un-had mace) and is invisible to every system. The stand nobody sees, available to everybody: accidentally the most Bohemian mechanic in the file (the Fold would see it; Skyrim can't).

### #135  "THE MIND OF MADNESS / SHEOGORATH"
  W1  THE DUNGEON IS A DIAGNOSIS
      Three rooms, three faculties, three failure modes of one documented mind — mental illness itemized into playable, READABLE spaces. Nothing else in the medium stages psychology this literally and this respectfully-under-the-jokes.
  W2  COMBAT VERBS REPURPOSED AS TREATMENT
      The cane's targets are symptoms and abstractions; every swing is an interpretive claim. Violence's grammar redirected into care without changing a single input.
  W3  THE PARANOIA ROOM VALIDATES THE PARANOIAC
      The threats WERE real — in the stands, mislocated. The quest's most humane read: the symptom wasn't delusion, it was mis-aimed accuracy. Strike the audience.
  W4  THE PATIENT IS NEVER THE TARGET
      Aim at tiny Pelagius and everything worsens — the design encodes therapy's first law as a targeting rule.
  W5  PERSISTENCE IS THE TERROR ROOM'S SOLVE
      Nightmares transform under treatment; the answer is staying with the changing thing through its changes. Iteration as care, mechanized.
  W6  THE KINDNESS IS SMUGGLED IN COSTUME
      The god who cannot say a sincere sentence is, structurally, the only being who visits the abandoned mad — the warmest fact in the file, never stated, always staged. Register as plausible deniability for grace.
  W7  THE HOOK IS THE ABANDONED DEVOTEE
      Entry through Dervenin's grief — madness's cost measured first in the people it leaves on the street holding a hip bone.
  W8  THE THRESHOLD IS INSTITUTIONAL AMNESIA
      A sealed palace wing: the capital's own filing-away of its emperor is the door you pick. The court hid him in death as in life; the quest's first lockpick is against a society's memory.
  W9  FORKLESSNESS MEANS ITERATION HERE
      The third single-door Daedric of the batch, and this one's narrowness reads as therapy's honest shape: no branches, just rooms revisited until they hold.
  W10 STABILIZED, NOT HEALED
      The mind is left quieter, not whole — and alone again, the god departing being the quest's own success condition. The bittersweet is structural: you were hired to end the only visit.

### #136  "THE LANDSMEET"
  W1  THE BOSS FIGHT IS A ROLL-CALL VOTE
      The civil war resolves as parliamentary procedure with an audible count — the medium's fullest staging of politics AS the climax rather than before it.
  W2  THE BALLOT WAS CAST WEEKS AGO
      Side quests as silent constituencies: the session renders prior state. Q102's phonebook-law at institutional scale — the finale is a ledger-read.
  W3  THE SAME WITNESS TESTIFIES BOTH WAYS
